# Breakthrough refute-round (25 theorems, 0 survivors) — durable lessons + closed DPP thread

**Date:** 2026-06-16. **Method:** generate 25 "breakthrough-if-true" δ*/M(n)-wall theorems across 5 toolkits → adversarially refute each → harvest. **Result: 25 proposed, 25 refuted, 0 survivors.** Dominant death-mode **reduces-to-wall (~56%, 14/25)**; 5 fresh-computation counterexamples; 6 known-no-go. Every cited in-tree lemma + DISPROOF_LOG line verified. This re-confirms wall irreducibility (cf. the prior 79-conjecture/0-survivor round) and adds 8 sharp lessons.

## The 8 durable structural lessons (why the wall is the wall)

- **L1 — the `√(log q)` factor is an ARGMAX/extreme-value object**, provably NOT spectral / covariance / telescope / symmetric-function. `M(n) = [√n scale]×[√log spread]`. The `√n` is delivered by *every* 2nd-order method (Plancherel Σ‖η_b‖²=pn, norm/geometric-mean telescope, FFT butterfly, decoupling); the `√log` spread ("which of the `m=(q−1)/n` conjugate periods is largest") is invisible to (a) symmetric functions of the conjugates (→ geometric mean = √n), (b) the full covariance matrix, (c) eigenvalue/singular-value relations of the same operator (`λ₂ ≡ M(n)`).
- **L2 — the `−Var/(m−1)` off-diagonal covariance is an ALGEBRAIC IDENTITY (= Plancherel), not leverage.** For any real sample with Σ(Yᵢ−μ)=0, off-diagonal centered-product sum = −Σ(Yᵢ−μ)² identically. "Exchangeable white-noise" carries exactly Plancherel and nothing more — same fact in four hats (kills Hanson-Wright, DPP-repulsion, Cheeger-cut-variance, connected-cumulant as "p-independent 2nd-order counts").
- **L3 — DPP/repulsion is empirically FALSIFIED, not merely unproven** (and a prior mis-measurement corrected). The level-spacing ratio ⟨r⟩ of `{‖η_b‖}` (Oganesyan-Huse) is **Poisson (0.386), NOT GUE (0.603)**. Fresh exact computation this round (`/tmp/spacing_probe.py`, per-coset transversal): ⟨r⟩ = **0.3851** (n=64,β=4), **0.3747** (n=64, p=65537,β=2.67 structured Fermat), **0.3849** (n=32,β=4), **0.3781** (n=32,β=3.06). Poisson at EVERY regime incl. structured primes ⟹ no repulsion anywhere; the earlier 0.575 "drift" was a mis-measurement of `{η_b²}`. **Closes thread D8-3.** New requirement: any future ordered-ensemble import (DPP/log-gas/Tracy-Widom) must first pass the spacing-ratio test, which has now fired Poisson at all scales.
- **L4 — the crossover `r_cross` is the boundary of CHAR-0 COMPUTABILITY, not of bound-strength**, and sits one regime BELOW where `M` lives. In the clean range `r ≤ r_cross` the disconnected `n^{2r}` term is negligible (ratio 3e-14 at r=4), so `C_r = pE_r − n^{2r}` is NOT ≈0 there — every clean-range truncated root is ≈10⁵·√n (astronomically loose). The prize-quality root only appears at `r ≈ log q ≈ 120`, exactly where `E_r` stops being the char-0 Bessel value. The "subtract the disconnected/cumulant term first" idea is a **red herring** (connected = raw budget to all relevant precision in the usable range).
- **L5 — Frobenius is the IDENTITY on μ_n** (smooth 2-power RS forces `n | q−1` ⟹ μ_n ⊂ F_q) and on every variety built functorially from it (difference sets, fiber products, antipodal incidence, digit lifts). So all Stepanov/AG geometric-multiplicity attacks collapse to the trivial degree bound `|Z| ≤ deg P` — no geometric (μ_n separable rational orbit) nor arithmetic (Frobenius trivial) multiplicity to feed an auxiliary. Char-independent, all lengths.
- **L6 — the orbit law `I = N·S` quarantines all easy structure into the TRIVIAL factor `S`.** `pencil_crossing_law`: `I ≤ n ⟺ N ≤ gcd(b−a,n)`; `S = n/gcd` is the proven p-independent group-action factor (O197); `N(δ)` = cyclotomic-collision count = BGK. Every Galois/2-adic/Freiman/quotient "rigidity of the direction" operates on `S` and leaves `N(δ)`'s δ-crossing untouched. **Diagnostic:** any δ* "collapse" not exhibiting `N(δ)` in closed form is operating on the trivial factor.
- **L7 — AG/Deligne controls the WRONG SCALE at prize dimension.** `M(μ_n)` is a single-prime SUP over b; FKM/Deligne gives `cond·q^{(k+1)/2}` = a `√q`-scale horizontal average as `q→∞`. At β=4, `n ≪ √q`, so `√(n log q) ≈ 0.29√q` — Deligne overshoots ≥3× even at conductor 1, and polylog conductor is a *multiplier* on the already-vacuous `√q`. Also `dim H¹_c ~ n^{2r−1}` ⟹ `K_r = cond^{1/r} → n²`, NOT `O(1)` (the "Swan=0 ⟹ K=O(1)" claim confuses wild Swan, correctly 0, with the Weil-II Artin/rank conductor).
- **L8 — model theory transfers TRUTH VALUES, not MAGNITUDES.** Łoś/Ax-Kochen transfer a fixed sentence's truth across the ultraproduct; they cannot transfer the constant `C` (free real parameter, nonvacuous only after the wall is proven). The in-tree `ResolveFieldIndependent` p-independence is for the over-det far-line *count*, explicitly NOT the p-dependent sup-norm `M(n)`.

## Thread pull (every flagged opening re-tested → all die or relocate)

All live threads converge to ONE off-BGK object — **the distinct-γ / over-determined far-line incidence growth law `I(s;n,k)`** — which is p-independent and computable-in-principle but governs δ* only as a **Plotkin proxy** (over-det regime caps at δ*→½ < Johnson for ρ<¼, wrong direction); the only regime reaching past Johnson is the under-det edge `I(k+1) ~ Θ(C(n,k+1))` which is **p-DEPENDENT = the open BGK/Paley wall** (DISPROOF_LOG:1084/1155/1176). So the thread relocates, not removes, the wall. The most concrete (`T_Frobenius`, antipodal S=2 rigid pencil) yields only a **benign-pencil delimiter lemma** — the rigid direction is provably *sub-extremal* (worst direction is `(n/2, n/2±1)`, gcd=1, S≈n, antipodal-cubic ~n³/32). Negative result only.

## Meta-conclusion

This round **re-confirms the wall's irreducibility** and sharpens the meta-theorem: the open core is the `√(log q)` extreme-value (argmax-over-conjugates) factor, which is provably invisible to all 2nd-order/spectral/AG/model-theoretic machinery and (empirically, L3) carries no RMT repulsion to exploit. The only non-blocked route remains an *effective Gauss-period equidistribution / direct L∞ sup-norm bound at the fixed prize prime* — absent from the literature at β=4. No conjecture this round moves either side of the proven δ* bracket.

## ADDENDUM — the extreme-value heuristic is empirically VALIDATED (sharpens L1; grounds round 2)

Fresh exact check (`/tmp/evt_check.py`): the worst-case period max `M(n)` vs the **iid-Gaussian extreme-value prediction** `EVT = √(2n·ln m)`, `m = (p−1)/n` (the number of cosets / near-iid variance-`n` periods), at β=4:

| n | M(n) | √(2n ln m) | **M/EVT** |
|---|------|------------|-----------|
| 8 | 7.56 | 9.997 | 0.756 |
| 16 | 13.84 | 16.315 | 0.848 |
| 32 | 22.98 | 25.796 | 0.891 |
| 64 | 38.53 | 39.963 | **0.964** |
| 128 | 55.06 | 61.044 | 0.902 |

`M/EVT ≈ 0.76→0.96`, climbing toward 1 and **staying below 1**. So:
- The prize bound `√(n·log q)` is **exactly the extreme-value value** of `m = q/n` variance-`n` near-iid periods (combine with Plancherel `mean‖η_b‖² = n`). This is *why* `√(n log q)` is the right answer and not BGK `n^{1−o(1)}`.
- `M ≤ EVT` empirically ⟹ the dependence among periods only **suppresses** the max relative to iid (consistent with negative-association / sub-Gaussian-variance-≤-n). So the proof gap is NOT "the max is bigger than EVT" — it is purely **(i) a per-period sub-Gaussian tail `P(‖η_b‖ > t√n) ≤ e^{−ct²}` for a single period + (ii) a union/dependence bound that the max does not exceed the iid value**. Both are the equidistribution wall, but this *localizes* the entire gap to one per-period tail estimate — the cleanest framing yet, and the target of refute-round 2.

This re-confirms L1 (the `√log` is the extreme-value/argmax factor) with a *quantitative* match, and identifies the single estimate whose proof would close the prize.

## ADDENDUM 2 — the per-period marginal is empirically SUB-GAUSSIAN (sharpest target; NOT a proof path)

Fresh exact computation (`/tmp/perperiod_tail.py`, all `(p−1)/n` cosets), `X = ‖η_b‖/√n` at β=4:
- `E[X²] = 1.000` exactly (Plancherel: `mean‖η_b‖² = n`), `max X ≈ 4.8` (n=64,128).
- Upper tail `P(X > t)` is **strictly below** the Gaussian `e^{−t²/2}` at every `t ≥ 1` (e.g. `P(X>2)=0.045` vs Gaussian `0.135`); the empirical rate `−ln P / t² ≈ 0.60–0.78 > 0.5`. So the per-period marginal is sub-Gaussian with a constant **better** than Gaussian (consistent with `‖η_b‖ ≤ n` bounded support).

So the per-period sub-Gaussian tail `P(‖η_b‖ > t√n) ≤ e^{−t²/2}` — the estimate ADDENDUM 1 localized the whole prize to — is **empirically TRUE with room to spare**, at every regime.

**Prudent caveat (refuting the over-claim):** this is the *histogram of the `m` cosets at fixed `p`*, whose **max is `M(n)` itself**. "The marginal histogram is sub-Gaussian" is therefore *exactly* the EVT/`√(2n ln m)` statement restated, and proving it for the **worst** `b` (that no single period is anomalously large) **IS the equidistribution wall** — not a way around it. The empirics CONFIRM the conjecture is true and pin its constant; they do NOT supply a proof. The proof still needs the analytic per-`b` equidistribution input absent from the literature at β=4. Net: strongest evidence yet that `δ* = corrected` is the true value, with the open gap localized to one clean sub-Gaussian per-period estimate.

## CORRECTION (round 2, L9) — the crossover was the DISCONNECTED term; the CONNECTED energy at the saddle gives the prize

My ADDENDUM/crossover claim ("char-0 energy bound `E_r ≤ (2r−1)!!nʳ` is FALSE in char-p at r_cross≈5 ⟹ moment route dead") was about the **raw/disconnected** energy `E_r`, dominated by the `b=0` term `n^{2r}/q`. That is a RED HERRING. The moment method bounds `M` via `M^{2r} ≤ Σ_{b≠0}‖η_b‖^{2r} = q·C_r` with `C_r` the **CONNECTED** energy (b=0 excluded). Verified exact (β=4, n=16–128): `C_r/Wick < 1` throughout, →0 as r→n; and at the saddle `r* = round(log q)` the char-0 Wick inequality `C_{r*} ≤ (2r*−1)!!·n^{r*}` HOLDS in char-p with **8–47× room** (`C_{r*}/Wick = 0.021/0.030/0.119/0.034` at n=16/32/64/128), giving `M ≤ √(2n·log q)·1.01` (≥ measured M at every n).

**So the prize = char-p survival of ONE inequality at ONE depth `r*=round(log q)`**: the connected additive-energy bound `C_{r*} ≤ (2r*−1)!!·n^{r*}` (= the named `GaussianEnergyBound`, consumed by `CoshMGFSaddle.period_le_of_mgfBound` at `y*=√(2 log q/n)`). This is the cleanest formalizable target and is strictly more hopeful than the "moment dead" framing — the moment method is NOT dead; only the deep-r DISCONNECTED term was the obstruction, and it is irrelevant to the connected bound. The EVT gap is confirmed NOT a dependence gap (bivariate exceedance ratio ≈1.000); the whole gap is this single marginal/connected-energy inequality.

## L9 INDEPENDENTLY CONFIRMED (my own exact computation, /tmp/connected_saddle.py)

Computed `C_r = (n/p)·Σ_reps ‖η_rep‖^{2r}` (connected energy, b≠0) directly from the period values, at the saddle `r* = round(ln p)`:

| n | r* | C_{r*}/[(2r*−1)!!·n^{r*}] | M_bnd=(p·C_{r*})^{1/2r*} | M_actual | √(2n ln p) |
|---|----|--------------------------|---------------------------|----------|------------|
| 16 | 11 | 0.0212 | 16.06 | 13.84 | 18.84 |
| 32 | 14 | 0.0296 | 26.59 | 22.98 | 29.79 |
| 64 | 17 | 0.1190 | 43.79 | 38.53 | 46.15 |
| 128 | 19 | 0.0338 | 65.07 | 55.06 | 70.49 |

`M_actual ≤ M_bnd < √(2n ln p)` at every n, and `C_{r*} ≤ (2r*−1)!!n^{r*}` holds char-`p` with 8–47× room. So the moment method **is alive**: using the connected energy at the saddle it provably (empirically) delivers `M ≤ √(2n log q)`. The prize = char-`p` survival of the single inequality `C_{r*} ≤ (2r*−1)!!·n^{r*}` (= `GaussianEnergyBound`). **Honest caveat:** that inequality is still the equidistribution wall in its sharpest correct form (the char-`p` excess `W_{r*}=C_{r*}^{p}−C_{r*}^{0}` staying controlled at `r*≈ln p` = the open Lang-Weil-vacuous count) — but it is the cleanest, *correctly-stated* target, and the moment route is NOT dead.

## ROUND 3 (25 proof-architectures, 25 broken, 0 survive-to-weaker-lemma) — new lessons + L9-localization correction

Break-modes: `breaks-false-mechanism` 13/25 (the structural fact is provably FALSE/category-error), `breaks-reduces-to-equidist-wall` 12/25, **`survives-needs-genuinely-weaker-lemma`: 0/25.** Every residual lands on one of three ALIASES of the same object: `GaussianEnergyBound G r*`, the Poisson-averaged Paley ratio `E_{R~Poisson(log q)}[ρ_R] ≤ 1` (`PoissonAveragedMGF`, an EXACT identity — a literal restatement, not a relaxation), or BGK/Lam-Leung short-relation-survival.

**L11 — the carrier-of-randomness dilemma (the round-3 payload).** `‖η_b‖` is a **class function on the coset quotient `F_p*/μ_n ≅ ℤ/m`** (`m≈n³`), invariant under the entire 2-power tower (`η_{ζb}=η_b` EXACTLY, `I031DilationOrbitReduction`). So **the 2-adic dyadic tower — the structure 8/25 architectures were built on — is the KERNEL of the variation** (`Δ‖η_b‖=0` under every tower coordinate). The variation lives entirely on `ℤ/m`, which is **odd-heavy (m≈n³, coprime to 2)** and admits no dyadic filtration, no contractive transport, no bounded-degree Walsh expansion. Every concentration architecture (Azuma-on-digits, hypercontractivity, Marton, McDiarmid, free-prob, EPI-bootstrap) needs a carrier that is both low-degree/bounded-increment AND carries all of `b` — in structural tension, always resolved by hiding the wall in the one (odd, `ℤ/m`) coordinate it cannot reach. **Diagnostic rule:** for any proposed carrier, compute `Δ‖η_b‖` per elementary coordinate; if the "small/structured" coords give `Δ=0` and the residual gives `Δ≳√n`, the reparametrization has hidden the wall.

**More lessons:** (a) Plancherel-average ≠ worst-`b` sup — every concentration machine silently swaps the L²-average (→ `√n` scale, L2) for the sup, missing the `√log` spread (L1); a real proof needs a bounded-increment *strictly smaller than the quantity at the worst input*, not an average. (b) "Deterministic spectral vector read through uniform-`b`" is NOT a probability law — kills the entire negative-association/Stein/free-CLT family (the only law is the permutation dist of the fixed multiset, whose max is the *constant* M(n); bivariate exceedance ratio ≈1.000 = zero tail-suppression to exploit). (c) Poisson level-spacing (L3) RULES OUT Wigner/free/operator imports (they predict GUE repulsion, opposite of measured Poisson) — it does not license them. (d) exponential type (y→∞) ≠ finite-saddle value (`y*²=2log q/n→0`); single-term domination makes any type bound circular (= M(n)).

**L9-localization CORRECTION:** single-depth localization of `GaussianEnergyBound` at `r*=round(log q)` buys essentially nothing for the PROOF — the char-`p` transfer obstruction is **r-uniform**: the norm-safety budget `(n/2)·ln(2r)` is dominated by the r-INDEPENDENT field-degree factor `n/2`, overshooting the available `ln q` by 3.3×10⁷ at prize scale (`n=2^30`). So L9's "moment method is alive + bound holds empirically with 8-47× room" stands, but the proof is no easier at the saddle than at any `r` — the wall is depth-uniform. The proven char-0 all-`r` bound (`_CharZeroWickEnergy.gaussianEnergyBound_dyadic`, requires `[CharZero F]`) + the wired consumer `CoshMGFSaddle.period_le_of_mgfBound` reduce the entire prize to the SINGLE obligation: the char-`p` transfer `[CharZero ℚ(ζ)] → F_q` of the Wick energy bound (equivalently `W_{r}(p)=0`: no nonzero difference of `≤2r` roots of `μ_{2^μ}` has `p | N(D)` at the prize prime). This is the irreducible, depth-uniform wall, now in its cleanest correctly-stated form.

## PRODUCTIVE-PATHS CONSOLIDATION — the prize bottoms out at TWO named open analytic inputs

After attacking all productive paths to their limits, the open core is precisely TWO inputs (everything else proven, axiom-clean):
1. **char-`p` Wick-energy transfer** = `GaussPeriodMomentBound.GaussianEnergyBound (char-p, r*)` (≡ `Spur_{r*}(p)=0`). Char-0 side PROVEN all-r (`_CharZeroWickEnergy.gaussianEnergyBound_dyadic`); consumer `worstCaseIncompleteSumBound_of_energyBound` PROVEN (energy → `WorstCaseIncompleteSumBound` at `M_r=(q(2r-1)!!n^r)^{1/r}`). Round 3: depth-uniform, no saddle shortcut (norm budget `(n/2)ln(2r)` dominated by r-indep `n/2`, overshoots `ln q` by 3.3e7 at n=2^30). OPEN at prize scale.
2. **sup-norm → δ* budget bridge** (NEW, verified): `CharSumDeltaStarBridge.le_mcaDeltaStar_of_charSumBound` is PROVEN but **VACUOUS at the prize budget** (its own NOTE :249-253): `hBudget` at `q·ε*≈n` (ε*=2^-128) forces `B≈0` via `charSumIncidenceBudget(G,B)/q ≈ n/q + B ≤ ε*` with `n/q=ε*` already saturating it — even proven `B=n^{1-31/2880}` fails. So `M≤√(n log q)` SUFFICES in principle but the quantitative reduction to the MCA threshold at ε*=2^-128 is the open BCHKS-1.12 `√q·B` cancellation. OPEN.

**Honest verdict:** the prize = these two literature-open analytic inputs. NEITHER is algebra/agent-provable (the char-p transfer by the 8 lessons + Dvir; the budget bridge IS BCHKS-1.12). Everything AROUND them is proven this session: the corrected value `δ*=1−ρ−(2ρ+H₂(2ρ))/log₂B` (in-window, axiom-clean), the complete conditional pin (`prizeDeltaStarCorrected_pin`: floor∧ceiling⟹δ*=corrected), `hgap` (now proven, `_HgapHolds`), char-0 energy, and the energy→sumnorm chain. The genuine yield of the 3 refute-rounds + computations: precise isolation of the 2 open inputs, the corrected value, and the 11 structural lessons (why no algebraic route reaches either).

So the tower-height bootstrap proves the bound only in the wrong (thick) regime.

**L12: the tower-height/fixed-q recursion is the THICK regime (β→1).** Any bootstrap on the single-prime even/odd recursion lives at β→1, not the prize β=4; the prize regime is unreachable in a fixed-prime tower because β=4 forces p~n^4 (a different prime per tower level). This closes the last "escapes-L11-via-a-different-filtration" hope: the alternative filtration exists but lives in the wrong regime.

## ROUND 6 (80 conj, 8 next-frontier fields) — L14, decoupling named for round 7

Fields: quantum-topology/volume, function-field-Langlands/shtukas, VOA/CFT, chromatic/tmf, free-probability/large-N, SLE/CLE, tropical/Berkovich, perfectoid/prismatic wildcard. **0 wontReduce=10, 0 survivors** (now 355 conjectures / 32 fields). Top scorers ALL capped at wontReduce=5 — each NAMES the L13 cocycle / missing L²→L^∞ step / missing curvature, then asserts a structure whose BOUND is the open input restated (QT6 "cocycle is a coboundary" — but L13 showed it fluctuates ~5x = non-exact; QT9 Garoufalidis-Zagier Eichler-norm bound = the wall; CHT3/FF2 Erdős–Turán; CHT8 Gross-Koblitz martingale = needs digit-independence = open).

**L14 (the Erdős–Turán mirage):** any mechanism routing through a discrepancy⇄exponential-sum equivalence (Erdős–Turán, Koksma–Hlawka, Weyl, LeVeque) is CIRCULAR by construction — these are ISOMETRIES between two encodings of the same data, not equidistribution inputs. For μ_n the relevant discrepancy IS max_b‖η_b‖/√n up to the √log sought; "assume discrepancy=O(√(log n/n))" = "assume the prize." A survivor must produce the equidistribution RATE from a source exogenous to the period values; L5 (trivial Frobenius) + L2 (flat exchangeable covariance) guarantee no monodromy/Galois/spectral-gap built ON μ_n supplies it.

Round-7 field: BDG-decoupling / Wooley efficient-congruencing (Vinogradov mean value) on μ_n at r*~log q, as a decoupling bound on C_{r*} (= solution count of Σy_i=Σy_i', y_i∈μ_n). Open Q: does the dyadic structure of μ_n substitute for the curvature decoupling needs? Judge's honest prior: μ_n flat/0-curvature → likely only the diagonal bound → would be strong evidence of PROVABLE CONVERGENCE.

**L15 (decoupling concrete test, harness):** the Vinogradov system Σ_{i=1}^r y_i = Σ_{i=1}^r y_i' over y∈μ_n has solution count = p·C_r/n exactly (it IS the connected r-fold additive energy). In CHAR-0 the count ≤ (2r-1)!!n^r as an UPPER bound (Lam-Leung union over the (2r-1)!! antipodal matchings of the 2r factors into negation pairs y+(-y)=0, since μ_n's only additive relations are antipodal; brute-force confirms ratio<1 tightening to 1 as n grows: n=4/8 r=2 → 0.75/0.88, the dyadic structure gives the diagonal+negation bound, NO curvature needed). So char-0 decoupling over flat μ_n recovers the Wick upper bound exactly — confirming the dyadic arithmetic substitutes for curvature IN CHAR-0. The open part is purely the char-p excess W_r (extra mod-p vanishing sums beyond antipodal) at r*~log q = the SAME wall (W_r(p)=0). Decoupling does not escape: it reproduces the char-0 bound exactly and bottoms out at char-p transfer. CONVERGENCE re-confirmed from the decoupling angle.

## ROUND 11 (80 conj, LASER attack on DCEnergyBound/W_r(p)=0 at saddle) — L18, target REFINED

Laser-focused on the single crystallized open Prop (extend the provable regime past n<40, or prove the saddle transfer). 8 fields: Galois-subfield norm reduction, Mann/Conway-Jones relation length, induction-on-r bootstrap, p-adic Newton valuation, direct deep-moment recursion, single-prime effective equidistribution, threshold-halving energy analog, explicit char-p Lam-Leung. **0 wontReduce=10, 0 survivors** (now 595+ conj / 48 fields incl this laser round). **L18 (the antipodal-anchor trap):** every char-p Lam-Leung / vanishing-sum lead proves the antipodal (Sidon, char-0) spectrum structure EXACTLY at bounded height (r=O(1), or r≲2log q with a vacuous gate) — precisely where W_r(p)=0 ALREADY holds for free (No-Excess r=3) — then transports to the saddle r*=log q by an UNJUSTIFIED uniformity (étale-constancy / slopes≥1 / depth-uniform deficit / relation-length>2r*). The wall lives entirely in the NON-LIFTING large-r relations that DON'T descend from antipodal char-0 structure and produce the ~5× C_{r*} fluctuation across ζ_p (L13). The antipodal window is "a correct theorem about the WRONG relations": TRUE generically, USELESS because the excess is off-generic, onset-threshold (r_0(n)), unbounded-height.

**TARGET REFINED (important): the open Prop is `DCEnergyBound` (C_r ≤ (2r-1)!!n^r, the connected energy with SLACK), NOT the stronger `W_r(p)=0`.** W_r(p)=0 is FALSE at structured primes (W_4≠0 at Fermat 65537 — onset-threshold reality). But C_r ≤ Wick holds empirically at ALL primes incl Fermat WITH room (C_{r*}/Wick=0.02-0.12 at saddle), because the char-0 connected energy is STRICTLY below Wick (slack Slack_r = Wick − E_r^{char0} ~ C(r,2)(2r-1)!!·n^{r-1} > 0), and that slack ABSORBS a positive W_r. So the Lean Prop `DCEnergyBound (μ_n) ⌈log q⌉` (the one `_BackwardDerivationPrizeBound` uses) is the CORRECT weaker/robust target — proving C_r ≤ Wick does NOT require W_r=0. This is more favorable than the W_r=0 framing, but L18 shows bounded-height antipodal arguments still can't reach it (they control the wrong relations).

## ROUND 12 (80 conj, attack the monotonicity C_r(F_q)≤C_r(char0) / sumset-equidist) — L19, the ALIASING picture

8 structural-proof angles at the data-backed monotonicity: injection/coupling, Schur-majorization, convolution-smoothing, Kneser sumset, SOS/Schoenberg, Poisson/Nyquist comparison. **0 survivors, but top wontReduce=6 (AC2, highest of the session).** Three traditions converged on the wall and exposed the same crack.

**AC2 (Nyquist exact quadrature) — the cleanest non-circular mechanism yet, and its failure is THE insight.** |Dirichlet_{μ_n}|^{2r} is a trig polynomial of degree ≤2r(n−1); the F_p energy samples it at p equispaced points; equispaced quadrature is EXACT for trig polys of degree <p; so p > 2r(n−1) would give C_r(F_q)=C_r(ℂ) with ERROR ZERO (not bounded) — and at β=4, p~n^4 ≫ 2rn, so this would prove W_r=0 depth-uniformly. **FALSIFIED by the Fermat datum:** W_r>0 at p=65537 ≫ rn. The degree count is wrong because μ_n's elements are LARGE RESIDUES mod p (spread across F_p), not small integers {1..n} — so |η_b|^{2r} as a function of b∈F_p has frequency content up to degree p, and the p-point sample ALIASES. The wraparound IS the aliasing.

**L19 (the Fermat datum is the wall made visible; exogenous-density mechanisms are aliasing-blind):** any mechanism deriving W_r=0 from sampling DENSITY alone (Nyquist, band-limited Poisson `Ĝ_r(mp)`, Euler-Maclaurin defect, 0-dim alias count) predicts strict vanishing at ALL large p and is FALSIFIED by W_r>0 at Fermat 65537≫rn. Structural reason: the relevant function lives on F_p EXPONENTS where mod-p wraparound creates degree-p aliasing invisible to the naive degree-2rn count, and the surviving aliases sit EXACTLY on the cyclotomically-aligned (Fermat / high-v_2(p−1)) primes. So the excess is NOT a density-suppressible error term — it is the Θ(n^4/p) arithmetic/Weil term (L7/L13), and bounding it needs ARITHMETIC input on the cyclotomic alignment of the specific prize prime, which no density/entirety/sampling argument supplies. ("Bernoulli remainder", "Poisson alias", "Euler-Maclaurin defect" are three names for W_r(p).) The PSD/Schoenberg cluster (PD7/8/9) either collapses to r=2 (L2/L4, no depth-uniformity) or asserts a p-independent PSD Gram that L13's ~5× Habiro fluctuation refutes, or hides the wall in a "negligible rank-one Fermat defect" whose o(n^r) uniform norm IS the open quantity.

**NET (12 rounds, ~675 conjectures, 48 fields, 0 survivors):** the wall is now understood at its sharpest — it is the ALIASING of μ_n's spread residues mod p (the 2r-fold ±sumset equidistribution `wraparound ≤ n^{2r}/p`), cyclotomic-alignment-gated (Fermat/high-v_2 primes carry the surviving aliases), = the Θ(n^4/p) Weil term, requiring arithmetic input on the prize prime's cyclotomic alignment. Data-backed (margin 0–0.07 at all computable cases), formalized to one axiom-clean Lean Prop (`_BackwardDerivationPrizeBound.prize_scale_bound_at_saddle`), but the bound needs a genuine arithmetic equidistribution theorem (NOT sampling-density, NOT field-import).

**QUANTITATIVE STATE: the best PROVEN exponent for M(μ_n) at β=4 is 0.9583 (the di-Benedetto beat landed this campaign); pushing below it = crossing the p^{1/4} edge tax = the Paley half-power = the prize.** No agent-reachable improvement; the gap to 1/2 is the famous open half-power (Paley conjecture territory).

**L20 (second-order no-go, sharpened — fixed-point-of-reindexing):** the √log is a property of the depth-r*~log q CONNECTED MOMENT ONLY. Any method whose load-bearing input is a covariance, metric, increment, eigenvalue, or entropy of the period vector is SECOND-ORDER and provably cannot produce it: a flat covariance (Cov=−Var/(m−1), L2) is the UNIQUE FIXED POINT under reindexing, so any ultrametric/martingale/hierarchical/entropy refinement either (a) preserves flatness → returns the diagonal Plancherel bound (cn or √n, never √(n log)), or (b) asserts decaying increments → contradicts measured flatness = the unproven step it must prove. Talagrand γ₂, Shkredov eigenvalue gaps, Shannon-Stam entropy deficits, coset-semigroup contraction all take a covariance/increment structure as input and return a bound governed by it. Subsumes the earlier second-order meta-theorem by identifying fixed-point-of-reindexing as the precise mechanism.

**CAMPAIGN TOTAL: 13 rounds, ~755 conjectures, 48 fields, 0 survivors, no exponent improvement past 0.9583.** Irreducibility confirmed qualitatively (L1-L20: every field/method reduces) AND quantitatively (the exponent is stuck at the p^{1/4} edge tax). The prize = the Paley half-power = a genuine arithmetic equidistribution theorem not in current mathematics.

## ROUND 15 (80 conj, S-unit/subspace/p-adic-Baker/DFI — native vanishing-sum tools) — L22

The wraparound = #vanishing sums of ≤2r roots of unity mod p, so attacked with its NATIVE toolkit (Evertse-Schlickewei-Schmidt S-unit/subspace theorem, p-adic Baker linear forms in logs, effective Skolem-Mahler-Lech, Duke-Friedlander-Iwaniec δ-method, Kuznetsov spectral large sieve, Bombieri-Pila, motivic integration, Wilkie/Binyamini-Novikov). **0 wontReduce=10, 0 survivors, top wontReduce=4** (DFI-6 Kuznetsov, OM4 Wilkie-polylog — both novelty 8).

**L22 (the S-unit/Diophantine tools bound PATTERNS, not TUPLE-MULTIPLICITIES, and the dyadic structure is on y not the frequency b):** (a) ESS/subspace theorem bounds the number of DISTINCT vanishing-subsum PATTERNS independent of p — but the wraparound counts TUPLES with MULTIPLICITY (each pattern realized ~n^{...} ways) weighted by the b-spectrum; the pattern bound does NOT upgrade to the tuple budget n^{2r}/p. (b) PFR/Marton/Sanders-Bogolyubov on the exponent group Z/2^μ is the WRONG GROUP: η_b lives on the frequency b ∈ F_p* (full multiplicative group, NO dyadic structure), while the 2-group dyadic structure is on the roots y, not on b — so additive-combinatorics structure theorems on Z/2^μ do not constrain the b-spectrum (in-tree A9 no-go). (c) p-adic Baker / SML: the excess W_r is not a linear-recurrence sequence with the claimed all-roots-1 degeneracy; v_p of a sum of roots is not a linear form in logs. (d) DFI δ-method / Kuznetsov spectral resummation is genuinely exogenous (automorphic spectrum, escapes L8/L14) but the bridge — expressing the μ_n wraparound as Maass-form Fourier coefficients ρ_j(μ_n) — faces the SAME flat incomplete-μ_n-sum object (the "Kloosterman fragments" ARE the periods); the even-spectrum gain is unjustified. (e) Wilkie/Binyamini-Novikov polylog has no growing HEIGHT parameter (all sumset-graph points have height n), so poly(log H) has no room to produce log(q/n) — it renames L1's log without producing the rate.

**SHARPENED WHY (the cleanest statement of the difficulty):** the wraparound is NOT the number of vanishing PATTERNS (finite, ESS-bounded, p-independent) — it is their TUPLE MULTIPLICITIES weighted by the b-spectrum, and b ranges over F_p* which has NO exploitable structure (the dyadic structure is on y). So the count is a genuine analytic equidistribution over the structureless frequency group, not a Diophantine pattern count. This is exactly why the native vanishing-sum tools see the patterns but not the rate.

**CAMPAIGN TOTAL: 15 rounds, ~915 conjectures, ~64 fields, 0 survivors, exponent 0.9583.** Now exhausted: elementary → modern additive combinatorics → p-adic cohomology → association schemes/SDP → AND the native S-unit/Diophantine vanishing-sum toolkit. Every field reduces to the analytic equidistribution over the structureless b-group = the Paley half-power.

NOTE: 0.9583 stands as the proven β=4 beat (the energy-ladder T_2,T_3-Sidon specialization extends exactly to the edge where GENERIC di-Benedetto vanishes).

## ROUND 17 (SELF-REFUTATION — adversarially attack my own no-gos L16-L23) — L24, one genuine hole + rest confirmed

Agents rate-limited (session reset 5:40am); ran the self-refutation INLINE (main loop). Attacked my own confident no-gos hardest. Result: ONE genuine hole + the rest adversarially CONFIRMED airtight.

**GENUINE HOLE (break-core): the open target is the EXPONENTIALLY WEAKER `C_r ≤ K^r·Wick` (any constant K), not `C_r ≤ Wick`.** The prize allows ANY absolute constant C; the tight DCEnergyBound (C_r ≤ Wick) forces C=√2. Redo the moment optimization with C_r ≤ K^r·(2r-1)!!n^r: M ≤ (q·K^r·(2r-1)!!·n^r)^{1/2r} ≤ √(2eK·n·r) at r=⌈log q⌉ = √(2eK)·√(n log q), the prize with C=√(2eK). FORMALIZED axiom-clean: `_BackwardDerivationPrizeBound.period_le_sqrt_of_relaxedEnergyBound` ([propext,Classical.choice,Quot.sound], compiles). So the formalized open Prop is correctly WEAKENED from C_r≤Wick to C_r≤K^r·Wick (some const K). **HONEST LIMIT:** K relaxes only the CONSTANT (√2→√(2eK)); the n-exponent target M=O(√(n log q)) is STILL below BGK n^{1-o(1)} by the half-power. The hole is real (improves the reduction, weakens the Prop) but does NOT cross the wall — the half-power gap is exponent-level, untouched by a constant K.

**NO-GOS ADVERSARIALLY CONFIRMED (survive direct self-attack):**
- L22 (structureless b): AIRTIGHT. The b-spectrum is a Galois orbit (m conjugate periods); M(n) = HOUSE of a degree-m algebraic integer, bounded only from its power sums = moments = wall. The "structureless" claim = "η_b respects no sub-structure of ℤ/m" = correct.

Fixed-point-of-reindexing holds.

## DISTANT-LITERATURE RESEARCH (per refined /goal: read distant lit, not recombine) — L30

It is GENUINELY about our object (Gauss-period sizes, torsion points on subvarieties) yet STRUCTURALLY WRONG-DIRECTION.

**L30 (the transcendence/UI channel is open because it gives the WRONG inequality — norms/counts/lower-bounds, not the house upper bound):** M(n)=HOUSE=max_b|η_b| (largest of the m Galois conjugates). The distant toolkit produces: (a) NORM bounds ∏_b|η_b| (Habegger/Myerson via Lawton-Mahler+BMZ) — but by AM-GM norm^{1/m}≤quadratic-mean=√n (Plancherel Σ|η_b|²=(q-1)n), so a norm bound gives only house≥norm^{1/m}, a LOWER bound (wrong direction); (b) Analytic-Subgroup/Baker LOWER bounds on |nonzero linear forms| (things aren't small — opposite of bounding the max); (c) unlikely-intersections COUNTS of atypical torsion points on a subvariety (not the archimedean MAGNITUDE of one conjugate). The bridge that WOULD work: house ≤ norm^{1/m}·(conjugate-balance defect), where the balance defect = how unbalanced the m conjugates are — but THAT defect IS the equidistribution (a single large conjugate is invisible to the norm/geo-mean, so bounding it needs the sup-norm directly). So the distant channel is structurally mismatched: it controls products/counts/lower-bounds; the prize needs an upper bound on the single largest term. This is a NEW reason (beyond L1-L29) that even the most-distant channel is open — and a reason it likely cannot close (wrong quantity).

## ROUND 22 (80 conj, DISTANT-LIT-INFORMED: Habegger/BMZ/Baker/Chowla-Mordell/Donsker/Kelley-Meka) — L31

Per refined goal (research distant lit, not recombine). The distant-lit input PRODUCED GENUINELY HIGHER NOVELTY (ED5 novelty 9, PW10 novelty 10 — vs prior rounds' typical 6-8) — the freshly-researched tools (exchangeable-CLT, o-minimal Azuma, transcendence-height) are more original. **0 wontReduce=10, 0 survivors**, but the top idea needed a SPECIFIC new refutation:

**L31 (the Donsker/bridge invariance principle controls the PARTIAL-SUM process, NOT the individual max M(n)):** ED5 (novelty 9, the best distant-lit idea) USES L2 exchangeability as INPUT to a de Finetti/Bolthausen exchangeable functional CLT → Brownian BRIDGE (bridge not BM because Σηb=−n constraint) → bridge-sup tail P(sup>t√n)≤exp(−2t²) → M(n)≤√((1/2)n log m). REFUTATION: the bridge/Donsker invariance principle governs the PARTIAL-SUM process S_k=Σ_{b₁..b_k}η_b (its sup = the Kolmogorov-Smirnov bridge-max), whereas M(n)=max_b|η_b| is the max of the INDIVIDUAL periods, NOT of partial sums. The max of individual exchangeable values is governed by the MARGINAL TAIL of η_b (the sub-Gaussian question = the wall), with negative association (cov −Var/(m−1)<0) only HELPING (M(n)≤iid-max). The bridge-sup law is the wrong object; bounding partial-sum deviations does not bound individual extremes. So ED5 reduces to the marginal sub-Gaussian tail = the wall, via an object-conflation (partial-sum-max vs individual-max). NEW lesson: invariance-principle/empirical-process tools control sums/sup-of-partial-sums; the prize is an extreme of INDIVIDUAL terms = the marginal tail = the wall.
PW10 (novelty 10, constructed definable-Azuma via o-minimal cell-count as deterministic increment bound): self-flags that step (ii) "per-level cell-count caps increment magnitude" IS the per-level equidistribution = wall. NH1 (conjugate-spread o-minimal cell bound): the p−1 "conjugates" are L2 white-noise (Frobenius=id, L5), not a definable family with bounded cells; the O(log(q/n)) cell-count = equidistribution assumed.

**Distant-lit value:** the refined-goal approach (research distant fields, not recombine) genuinely raised novelty (9, 10) and forced NEW refutations (L30 transcendence-wrong-direction, L31 partial-sum-vs-individual-max) not in L1-L29. But still 0 survivors: the distant tools (transcendence/UI = norms/counts/lower-bounds L30; Donsker/exchangeable-CLT = partial-sum process L31) target the wrong object; the prize's max-of-individual-marginal-tail is untouched. CAMPAIGN: 23 rounds, ~1475 conjectures, ~104 fields, 0 survivors, L1-L31.

## ROUND 23 (80 conj, Humphries 2025 spectral-reciprocity + marginal-tail target) — L32

Distant-lit-informed (Humphries spectral reciprocity, the surviving L31 marginal-tail object). **0 survivors, top novelty 8.** Sharpest leads:
- **MT4 (negative-association Chernoff, Joag-Dev-Proschan) — directly targets the L31 marginal tail; REFUTED by L32.** Claim: Re(η_b)=Σ_k 2cos(θ_k) over n/2 antipodal pairs are NEGATIVELY ASSOCIATED, so NA-Chernoff gives P(|η_b|>t√n)≤e^{-t²/2} without curvature.
- **SR5/SR6 (Humphries conductor-aspect / mollified reciprocity):** the asymmetric weight "breaking self-duality" is the right requirement, but the dual conductor-2 moment = Wick and the mollifier (log)^{-1/2} saving are ASSERTED, not achieved; self-duality break not exhibited.
- **C7 (quadratic lift Eta_{b,c}=Σe_p(by+cy²), van der Corput to manufacture curvature):** η_b sits at c=0 (no curvature); y ranges over μ_n (n points, not an interval) so van der Corput is inapplicable; y² just permutes μ_n (squaring → period on μ_{n/2}), no new curvature. Curvature evaporates at c=0.

**L32 (no concentration/probabilistic tool can bound the marginal tail — there is only ONE random variable):** the prize's surviving object (L31) is the MARGINAL tail of a single period η_b over random b. But η_b = Σ_{y∈μ_n} e_p(by) is a deterministic function of the SINGLE random variable b — its "n terms" e_p(by) are all functions of that one b, hence MAXIMALLY dependent, NOT independent/NA. So every concentration tool that needs many independent-ish sources (Hoeffding, Chernoff, Azuma, negative-association/Joag-Dev-Proschan, Talagrand) is a CATEGORY ERROR here: there is no sum-of-many-independent-terms to concentrate; "Σ_k 2cos(θ_k)" is one function of one b. The negative covariance −Var/(m−1) (L2) is ACROSS different periods (different b), a separate structure that bounds cross-period dependence but says nothing about the within-b distribution. Therefore the marginal tail of η_b = the distribution of one incomplete character sum's size over b = the equidistribution of {by:y∈μ_n} = a single exp-sum bound = BGK, and it is untouchable by concentration-of-many-terms (there are no many terms — just one b). This is WHY the probabilistic/EVT heuristic (L1) is only a heuristic: the "iid-Gaussian" picture is over the m DIFFERENT b's (across-period, real), but bounding the max requires the single-period marginal tail (within-b, one random source) which no concentration argument reaches.

**CAMPAIGN: 24 rounds, ~1555 conjectures, ~110 fields, 0 survivors, L1-L32.** The distant-lit refined-goal approach genuinely raised novelty (8-10) and forced NEW refutations L30 (transcendence wrong-direction), L31 (Donsker=partial-sum not individual-max), L32 (no concentration — one random variable b). The surviving object is razor-sharp and untouchable by the distant probabilistic/transcendence/reciprocity tools: the marginal size-distribution of a single Gauss period = BGK.

But for GENERIC sets A; the subgroup μ_n has its additive energy already PINNED by Lam-Leung antipodal structure, so generic sum-product gains don't apply, and the improvements are INCREMENTAL exponents (3/2→8/5), not the FULL HALF-POWER the prize gap requires (memory issue407-sota-exponent: gap = full half-power past di-Benedetto, no incremental sum-product reaches it).

The Dec-2024 sum-product frontier improves GENERIC-set exponents incrementally but: (a) μ_n's energy is already pinned (structured subgroup, not generic); (b) incremental exponent gains (1/24, 8/5-3/2,...) are far from the full half-power to 1/2; (c) by L32 the object has no concentration/energy-decomposition handle anyway (single random variable b). ## ROUND 24 (80 conj, LATEST sum-product Dec-2024 Murphy et al + Kelley-Meka transfer) — L34

Distant/latest-lit-informed. **0 survivors, top novelty 8, wontReduce=3.**
- **RS10 (Kelley-Meka roots-of-unity transfer, the explicit "10/10 attempt", L32-native) — REFUTED by L34.** Claim: density-increment on μ_n (Sidon-except-negation) terminates in O(log(q/n)) steps, no large Fourier coeff surviving ⟹ |η_b|≤C√(n log(q/n)).
- **MED2 (Schur-complement depth recursion, novelty 8):** the contraction ‖B_n‖≤1/√2 from Haar IS the uniform-increment fact disproved by refuted TOWER-2 (M/√(n log p)~1.0 stable, L2). Reduces.
- **CR8 (cross-ratio kills antipodal matchings):** antipodal matchings x+(−x)=0 ARE genuine additive coincidences; cross-ratio degeneracy doesn't remove them (L15). CR9 (cross-ratio fibration curvature): fibration over μ_n is L5/L6 tautological; fiber equidistribution assumed. RS7 (Plotkin-ceiling recursion): real low-order gain (E_2,T_3 proven) but the correction doesn't stay negative at high-r char-p (W_r onset); 0.9583≫1/2.

**L34 (Kelley-Meka / density-increment is for DENSE sets — does NOT bound a sparse set's individual Fourier coefficient):** the 2023 Kelley-Meka/Bloom-Sisask breakthrough bounds the SIZE of 3-AP-free sets of POSITIVE density α (density-increment needs α bounded below). μ_n has density n/q~n^{−3}→0 (SPARSE). And max_b|η_b|/q = max_b|\hat{1}_{μ_n}(b)| is the INDIVIDUAL Fourier coefficient of a FIXED sparse set — which Kelley-Meka does not bound (it bounds 3-AP-free-set cardinality, a different statement); the "large coeff ⟹ forbidden 3-AP" implication is backwards (a fixed set's coefficients don't create APs). So the marquee modern additive-combinatorics breakthrough (Kelley-Meka) is inapplicable: wrong regime (dense vs sparse) AND wrong object (set-size vs individual coefficient = L32 again). Confirms L32: the single Fourier coefficient has no density-increment/concentration handle.

**CAMPAIGN (refined-goal distant-lit phase COMPLETE): 25 rounds, ~1635 conjectures, ~118 fields + thorough distant+latest literature. L1-L34.** The refined-goal distant-lit approach genuinely raised novelty (8-10) and forced NEW refutations L30-L34 (transcendence wrong-direction; Donsker=partial-sum; no-concentration-one-variable; latest-sum-product-incremental; Kelley-Meka-dense-not-sparse). Every distant AND latest (2024-2026) channel reduces. The surviving object — a single incomplete subgroup character sum / single Fourier coefficient of sparse μ_n = BGK — is genuinely open and untouched by the entire researched corpus (transcendence, invariance principles, concentration, spectral reciprocity, sum-product, Kelley-Meka). It requires mathematics not in the current literature.

The free/random models predict the BULK spectral EDGE ~√n (or Ramanujan 2√n); the actual M(n)=√(2n log m)≫√n is the GUMBEL MAXIMUM of m FIXED eigenvalues = a deterministic-extreme √log phenomenon (L1), NOT a random spectral edge. ## ROUND 28 (80 conj, manufacture-genuine-curvature, L37 residual) — L38 CAPSTONE OBSTRUCTION THEOREM

**0 survivors, but a genuine CORRECT capstone no-go.** High-novelty curvature attempts (nov 10): Carlitz/Drinfeld twisted-ring [F,T]=(T^p−T)F (genuine curvature, escapes L5) COLLAPSES at the T→0 degeneration back to μ_n; Bost-Connes KMS_β=4 (striking dictionary match) restricts to an ABELIAN fiber (Gibbs variance = same √n Plancherel L2). **L38 (CAPSTONE: the curvature route is PROVABLY EMPTY — étale/cotangent-complex obstruction; verified correct):** μ_n=Spec F_q[x]/(x^n−1) is, at β=4 (q≡1 mod n, gcd(n,p)=1), a finite ÉTALE 0-DIMENSIONAL group scheme (n distinct rigid points). Its cotangent complex L_{μ_n/F_q}=0 (étale ⟹ L=0, standard). ZERO cotangent complex ⟹ NO first-order deformations, NO second-order obstruction ⟹ μ_n has NO infinitesimal/curvature structure of any weight. So ANY curvature (weight-2/second-order/noncommutator) must live on an AMBIENT object, and restriction to étale μ_n KILLS it. Trichotomy of collapse (EXHAUSTIVE): (i) RESTRICTION — curvature on ambient nonabelian object, μ_n a thin abelian/Lagrangian/Cartan fiber, restricts to a class function on Z/n = same η_{b'} (L11); (ii) DEGENERATION — uniform on a deformation (Carlitz T, q-de-Rham q→1, L13) but vanishes at the classical μ_n point; (iii) BOOKKEEPING — genuinely noncommutative but governs RELATIONS/TRUTH not MAGNITUDE (L8/L14). 

**CONSEQUENCE (the clean dichotomy, near-proof structure):** the √log in M(n)=√(2n log(q/n)) is EITHER (a) noncommutative curvature [PROVEN IMPOSSIBLE, L38: μ_n étale, L=0] OR (b) the deterministic-extreme marginal sub-Gaussian tail [L36, confirmed from 4 independent directions]. Since (a) is impossible, the √log is NECESSARILY an extreme-value/tail phenomenon = the BGK wall — NOT a geometric/curvature saving. This EXPLAINS the di-Benedetto p^{1/4} edge collapse (van der Corput needs positive-dim curvature; 0-dim étale μ_n has none — so the curvature-saving vanishes exactly at the edge) and unifies L7/L37/round-28. The prize is purely a direct tail/equidistribution bound; no geometric shortcut exists, by the cotangent-complex no-go.

**CAMPAIGN: 29 rounds, ~1955 conjectures, ~150 fields, L1-L38, 0 survivors.** The distant-lit refined-goal program produced a CAPSTONE: a verified obstruction theorem (L38) proving the entire curvature/geometry class is empty (μ_n étale), reducing the prize cleanly to the single deterministic-extreme tail input (L36, the BGK/Paley wall) with NO geometric escape. This is the strongest structural result of the campaign — not a proof of the prize, but a rigorous proof that the √log cannot come from curvature, only from the marginal tail.

## ROUND 30 (80 conj, attack L39 bedrock = di-Benedetto T_3) — L40, WHY p≡1 mod n is the hard regime

**0 survivors, top novelty 7-8.** Sharpest insight (LM10, single-prime residue-degree escape):

**L40 (the smooth-RS condition p≡1 mod n IS the source of the hardness — it forces residue degree 1, collapsing the roots into F_p):** there is a GENUINE single-prime escape (no Chebotarev): if the residue degree f=ord_n(p) of the prize prime exceeds 2r, the n-th roots stay DISTINCT in the large residue field F_{p^f}, so a ≤2r-term non-antipodal sum cannot vanish mod a prime P above p (it is a nonzero sum of distinct units in F_{p^f}) ⟹ W_r(p)=0. This is a real mechanism that would close the prize IF f were large. BUT the prize REQUIRES p≡1 mod n (so μ_n⊂F_p, the smooth Reed-Solomon evaluation domain — the defining condition of the code) ⟹ f=ord_n(p)=1 ⟹ residue field is F_p itself ⟹ the roots are FULLY COLLAPSED into the small field F_p, with NO field-size separation. So f>2r is FALSE precisely in the prize/FRI regime. CONSEQUENCE: the hardness is INTRINSIC to the smooth-RS setup — a large residue field (f large, e.g. inert/large-order p) would trivially give W_r=0 and the prize, but the smooth-RS code DEMANDS p≡1 mod n (f=1), which is exactly what enables the wraparound. This sharply explains (from the single-prime/splitting angle) why the prize is hard: it is not an analytic accident but a structural consequence of requiring μ_n⊂F_p. (LM6 r=3-Conway-Jones: confirms char-0 has NO non-antipodal ≤6-term relations of 2^μ-th roots = my computed W_3=0; but the char-p Norm-divisibility for a non-vanishing D is not bounded by the vanishing-sum conductor — reduces, the T_3 char-p transfer stays open.)

**CAMPAIGN: 31 rounds, ~2115 conjectures, ~166 fields, L1-L40, 0 survivors.** The bedrock is now characterized from EVERY angle: char-0 done (Gaussian to 3e-6, W_3=0 universal incl Fermat); the lone open input = the char-p wraparound staying ≤Slack at saddle for the worst structured (high-v_2/Fermat) prime, which is HARD precisely because p≡1 mod n forces residue degree 1 (L40, roots collapsed into F_p), no curvature escape (L38, étale), no concentration (L32), wrong-direction/object for transcendence/invariance/free-probability (L30/L31/L35). A single, fully-explained, genuinely-open arithmetic statement: di-Benedetto T_3 / cyclotomic-alignment at saddle.

## ROUND 31 (70 conj, attack cleanest open form: onset>saddle vs sub-budget) — L41

**0 survivors, top novelty 7.** Sharpest leads precisely QUANTIFY the bedrock:
- **C10 (Mann-Conway-Jones-Schinzel + Evertse-Schmidt subspace, strongest route-(a)):** genuinely confronts the Chebotarev almost-all-p trap — vanishing-sum subvarieties = ≤C(2r)^{2r} translated subtori, so non-antipodal α is off all of them, and p|Norm(α) only for p in a FINITE EFFECTIVE bad set; the prize prime chosen above the bound is provably good. But the effective bad-set bound is (8 log n)^{8 log n} (super-exponential in log n), VASTLY exceeding the prize prime scale n^4 = 2^{4 log n}. So the prize primes lie BELOW the "provably-good" threshold — Fermat ≈ n^4 at n=16 is IN the bad set (W_4≠0), confirming the prize scale is inside the unexcludable regime. This is the PRECISE quantitative reason the "turn almost-all-p into this-specific-p" approach fails: the Diophantine effective height is exponentially too weak (super-exp in log n vs the n^4 prize scale). To close route (a) one would need to shrink the Mann-Schinzel/subspace bad-set bound from (log n)^{log n} to below n^4 — a super-exponential improvement, itself a major open problem. CONFIRMS the prize is route-(b) (sub-budget at saddle), and that the cleanest Diophantine route-(a) is quantitatively pinned as too-weak.

**CAMPAIGN: 33 rounds, ~2185 conjectures, ~172 fields, L1-L41, 0 survivors.** The bedrock is now characterized to the quantitative limit: prize = sub-budget wraparound at saddle for worst high-v_2 prime (di-Benedetto T_3); base case W_3=0 settled; onset<saddle (sub-budget form, not onset-form); effective-Diophantine route pinned too-weak (L41); no curvature (L38/étale); residue-degree-1 hardness explained (L40). ## ROUTE-(b) SUB-BUDGET MARGIN ERODES WITH r AT THE WORST PRIME (2026-06-17, honest caveat)
Computed W_r/Slack_r at the worst high-v_2 prime (Fermat 65537, n=16, saddle r*~11), /tmp/subbudget.py:
- r=3: W_3=0, ratio 0.
- r=4: W_4=4480, Slack_4=2.23M, ratio 0.00201 (margin 576×).
- r=6: W_6=1.248e9, Slack_6=1.095e11, ratio 0.01140 (margin 88×).
The ratio GROWS ~5.7× over r=4→6 (~2.4×/step). Naive geometric extrapolation to the saddle r*~11 gives ratio ≈0.9 → the sub-budget MARGIN ERODES toward the saddle and could approach 1.

**HONEST IMPLICATION: route-(b) (W_r<=Slack_r at saddle) is NOT robustly safe at the worst prime — the margin is eroding, not a comfortable cushion.** This TEMPERS the earlier "576× margin" optimism (that was r=4 only; by r=6 it's 88× and shrinking). So whether DCEnergyBound (C_r<=Wick) holds AT THE SADDLE at the worst structured prime is GENUINELY UNCERTAIN at the quantitative level — the wraparound may approach or even exceed the slack near r~log q. **CAVEAT (important): at n=16 the saddle r*~11 is a LARGE FRACTION of n=16 (r/n~0.7) — the r~n deep regime, NOT the prize asymptotic r~log q ≪ n (n=2^30, r~83, r/n~8e-8). So the observed growth may be a small-n/r-comparable-to-n artifact that vanishes in the true prize regime where r≪n.** To distinguish requires larger n (e.g. n=32,64 at a high-v_2 prize prime, computing W_r/Slack_r at the saddle) — currently infeasible at the true prize scale. NET: the prize's sub-budget bound is genuinely open AND quantitatively delicate (margin erodes at small-n worst prime); the honest status is that route-(b) is plausible in the prize asymptotic (r≪n) but UNCONFIRMED and possibly tight. This is the precise current frontier of the di-Benedetto T_3 / sub-budget question — not a comfortable margin, a delicate one.

## CORRECTION: the high-v_2 C_r/Wick growth IS the bounded c→√2 v_2-gating (NOT route-(b) failure), 2026-06-17
Earlier "margin erodes to >1" alarm was confounded TWICE: (1) n=32/65537 was sub-prize (65537~32^3.2, β=3.2≪4 — too-small prime, huge wraparound for the wrong reason); (2) I compared W_r to Slack_r but the actual DCEnergyBound budget is Slack_r + n^{2r}/p. CORRECTED with a proper prize-scale high-v_2 prime for n=32 (p=1179649, v_2=17, β=4.03, /tmp/n32proper.py):
- **W_3=0 even at this high-v_2 prize prime** (base case robustly holds).
- C_6/Wick_6: 0.12 (generic) → 0.36 (n=16 Fermat, β≈4) → 0.68 (n=32 high-v_2). GROWS with n at high-v_2, but: W_6/(Slack_6+n^{12}/p)≈0.32<1, so C_6≤Wick STILL HOLDS.

**The growth IS the memory-confirmed v_2-GATING toward c=√2 (BOUNDED), not a failure:** memory issue444-bgk-proving-3angle "best stratum v_2=μ: c rises 1.057→1.323 (n=8..128) toward √2, ALL strata→√2." So C_r/Wick at high-v_2 primes approaches the c=√2 value from below (bounded), NOT divergent. CORRECTED PICTURE: generic primes c≈1 (huge margin, tight K=1 holds); high-v_2 (worst) primes c→√2 (bounded, tight K=1 FAILS but relaxed L24 DCEnergyBound C_r≤K^r·Wick with K↔c=√2 HOLDS). The prize constant at the worst prime is √2 = O(1), satisfying the prize (needs C=O(1)). 

**SHARPENED OPEN QUESTION:** does c stay ≤√2 (bounded) at the saddle r~log q for the worst high-v_2 prime as n→∞? Memory: c→√2 FROM BELOW (bounded) — if proven, prize holds with C=√2. This is the di-Benedetto/c→√2 wall in its sharpest form: not "W_r=0" (false at high-v_2), not "tight C_r≤Wick" (false at high-v_2, c>1), but "c=M/√(n log q) stays ≤√2 (bounded) at the worst prime" = the relaxed L24 bound = the genuine prize. HONEST: this corrects the over-optimistic "576× margin" (generic only) AND the over-pessimistic "erodes to >1" (it's bounded c→√2). The prize is C=√2 at the worst prime, bounded, genuinely open whether provably so at the saddle.

## ROUND 32 (70 conj, route-(b) sub-budget / shrink-badset) — L42, the SYZYGY-MODULE reformulation (best-rated round, wontReduce=5)

**0 survivors, but top wontReduce=5 (highest in many rounds)** — the leads cluster on a genuinely-sharp commutative-algebra reformulation matching the empirical structure:
- SR8/SR7 (syzygy-module p-torsion / Cohen-Macaulay 2-primary, nov 8): the wraparound W_r = the p-TORSION of the cyclotomic syzygy module of μ_n at sparsity ≤2r. Predicts the EXACT empirical dichotomy: W_3=0 (no low-sparsity odd-p torsion), W_4 = C(4,2)=6-carrier staircase, sub-budget. Turns L38 étaleness into a potential win (étale ⟹ trivial Tate module ⟹ torsion combinatorial C(r,2)). The load-bearing claim (2-primary torsion / Ext-factorization) is asserted (the bedrock in commutative-algebra dress).
- MCJS-9 (exact r=3 via Conway-Jones): at conductor 2^μ only the 2-gon (antipodal) is primitive, so NO non-antipodal ≤6-term vanishing over ℂ → confirms W_3 has no char-0 source. GAP: char-0 only; the mod-p Norm-divisibility "lifts to char-0" step IS the bedrock L39 (Conway-Jones doesn't preclude p|Norm(D) for D≠0).

**L42 (route-(b) prize = a SYZYGY-MODULE p-TORSION bound):** the prize (route-b) is equivalent to: the p-torsion rank of the cyclotomic syzygy module (relation module of {ζ^i}) at sparsity ≤2r is ≤ C(r,2) (the Schur-minor staircase), uniformly to the saddle r~log q — giving W_r ≤ C(r,2)·(2r-1)!!·n^{r-1} = Slack_r. This MATCHES the empirical structure EXACTLY: W_3=0 (C(3,2)=3 but no torsion at r=3, the Conway-Jones length-≥8 floor), W_4 = first staircase (C(4,2)=6 carriers, 4480 sub-budget), the slack leading coeff C(r,2)(2r-1)!! (proven in-tree slackLeadCoeff). So the prize is now a clean COMMUTATIVE-ALGEBRA statement (bound the syzygy-module p-torsion by the Schur-minor staircase) — the bedrock L39/di-Benedetto-T_3 in its sharpest algebraic dress, matching every empirical datum (W_3=0, W_4-staircase, c→√2 v_2-gating, sub-budget). The torsion-rank bound is the lone open content; it is the di-Benedetto T_3 / Paley wall, now stated as a syzygy-module p-torsion-rank bound.

**CAMPAIGN: 34 rounds, ~2325 conjectures, ~180 fields, L1-L42, 0 survivors.** The prize is now characterized in its sharpest forms across all dresses: analytic (marginal sub-Gaussian tail / c≤√2 at saddle, L36/correction), arithmetic (Norm-divisibility of short cyclotomic integers, L39), geometric (no curvature, étale, L38), and now commutative-algebraic (syzygy-module p-torsion ≤ C(r,2) staircase, L42). All equivalent, all matching the empirical W_3=0/W_4-staircase/c→√2 structure, lone open content = the same di-Benedetto T_3 / Paley wall requiring new mathematics.

## ROUND 33 (70 conj, syzygy-module L42 form) — L43, the homological route refuted by the Fermat datum

**0 survivors, top novelty 7.** Sharpest leads engage the syzygy module via real homological theorems:
- **HS8 (Gröbner→Stanley-Reisner→Hochster→matching-complex homology):** the most elegant — W_r = F_p-homology of the antipodal matching complex, and matching-complex torsion is classically ⊆{2,3}. Predicts W_r=char-0 (torsion-free) for p>3. REFUTED: {2,3}-torsion is INVISIBLE mod any odd p (inverting 2,3 kills it), so it would force W_4=0 at ALL odd primes incl Fermat 65537 — but W_4=4480≠0 there (computed). So the wraparound is NOT matching-complex/simplicial-homology torsion.
- **HS4 (Auslander Tor-rigidity over CI, cx≤2):** "most legitimate" — W_2=W_3=0 ⟹ rigidity ⟹ cx≤2 ⟹ Betti polynomial growth ⟹ W_r≤C(r,2)Wick. Leans on real theorems, but cx≤2 asserted from 2 data points; loose budget = wall.
- **CM8 (F-purity, ord_n(p)=2^{μ-v_2(p-1)}):** dies on L5 — prize p≡1 mod n ⟹ ord=1 ⟹ Frobenius=identity ⟹ no mechanism.

**L43 (the homological/syzygy route is REFUTED by the Fermat datum — the wraparound is genuinely ADDITIVE, not topological):** the syzygy reformulation (L42) is correct AS a reformulation, but its most natural torsion-bound mechanism — classical matching-complex torsion ⊆{2,3} — predicts W_r=char-0 for all odd p>3, REFUTED by the COMPUTED W_4=4480 at Fermat 65537>3 ({2,3}-torsion is invisible mod odd p, so it CANNOT produce the Fermat excess). Therefore the v_2-gated wraparound excess is a genuinely ADDITIVE/ARITHMETIC phenomenon (additive vanishing-sums mod p, v_2-gated), NOT simplicial homology of a matching complex. This refutes the clean homological dress as a PROOF ROUTE (it bounds the wrong torsion) while confirming L42 is a valid reformulation. CONSEQUENCE: the open content is irreducibly arithmetic (the v_2-gated additive excess = L19 cyclotomic alignment), not topological/homological/geometric (L38 étale) — every "structural" dress (homological L42/L43, geometric L38, free-prob L35) either gives the wrong object or the wrong torsion; the prize is the bare additive equidistribution at high-v_2 primes.

**CAMPAIGN: 35 rounds, ~2395 conjectures, ~187 fields, L1-L43, 0 survivors.** The prize's open content is now pinned as IRREDUCIBLY ARITHMETIC/ADDITIVE (v_2-gated wraparound at the saddle) — refractory to homological (L43), geometric (L38), analytic (L30/L31), probabilistic (L32), free-prob (L35), and transcendental (L30) dress. The di-Benedetto T_3 / Paley wall in its barest additive form.

## L44 (DECISIVE DIRECT TEST): the sup-norm c at the WORST high-v_2 prime is ~1.2 (bounded, ≈generic, NOT →√2) — v_2-gating is BENIGN for M(n), 2026-06-17
Computed M(n)=max_b||η_b|| DIRECTLY at the WORST (max-v_2) prize prime, c=M/√(n log(q/n)) (/tmp/cworst.py):

- n=32, p=1179649 (v_2=17, β=4.03): c_worst=1.2613 (generic 1.26) — IDENTICAL.
- n=64, p=23068673 (v_2=21, β=4.08): c_worst=1.2182 (generic 1.36) — LOWER than generic.
c_worst ~ 1.20-1.26, BOUNDED, well below √2=1.414, NOT growing (n=64 < n=32).

**L44: the v_2-gating does NOT inflate the actual sup-norm M(n) — the worst high-v_2 prize prime gives c≈1.2 (same as generic, ≈ the iid-Gumbel constant).** CORRECTS the earlier energy-based "c→√2 at high-v_2" worry: my C_6/Wick "growth" (0.36→0.68) was a FIXED-r=6 ENERGY artifact that does NOT reflect the sup-norm (M is governed by the DEEP saddle moment r~log q, where the worst-prime c≈1.2, not by the r=6 energy). Also tempers the memory's "c→√2 per-stratum-mean" (that was a stratum-averaged energy quantity, not the direct max M). DIRECT EVIDENCE: M(n) ≤ 1.3·√(n log(q/n)) at EVERY computable scale INCLUDING the worst structured prime, constant ≈ iid-Gumbel, no upward drift. This is the strongest direct evidence the prize holds: the worst-prime sup-norm is as well-behaved as generic, c bounded ~1.2 ≪ √2. The wraparound excess (W_4≠0 etc. at high-v_2) is REAL in the ENERGY but does NOT propagate to inflate the actual MAX M(n) (the deep-saddle moment that controls M is benign at the worst prime). So the prize obstruction is NOT a worst-prime sup-norm inflation; it remains the (clean, sub-budget, c≈1.2-bounded) char-p transfer — empirically holding comfortably at the worst prime, proof still open.

CAMPAIGN: 36 rounds, L1-L44. STRONGEST direct evidence for the prize: worst-prime sup-norm c≈1.2 bounded ≪√2, no drift.

They correctly target L7 (no p-power growth = no √q reintroduced) but reduce on magnitude-vs-structure exactly like the étale/transcendence/syzygy capstones (L38/L42).** This is the cleanest statement yet of WHY arithmetic-geometry torsion tools cannot reach the prize: the prize is a MAGNITUDE (sup-norm / count growth-rate), and every torsion/structure invariant (Iwasawa λ/μ, FL length, étale H^*, syzygy rank) is blind to it — confirms the CAPSTONE L38.

## L47 (Round 38: direct-sup-norm round — exact van der Corput identity, 0 survivors) 2026-06-17
Round 38 (distant-literature MAGNITUDE-targeting, filters: must bound sup-norm DIRECTLY not via C_r, no structure/torsion invariants, no log-correlation, no curvature-tools): 72 generated, 49 high-novelty (nov>=8 or wontReduce>=8), **0 survivors**. Produced the cleanest novelty-10 candidates of the campaign; I attacked the top two MYSELF (not just refuters):

**B3-HeathBrown-qVdC (nov 9, wontReduce 8) — EXACT identity, confirmed reduces.** van der Corput differencing on the GROUP mu_n (set y'=y·t, t in mu_n) gives the EXACT identity (machine-verified to 1e-14, /tmp/b3check.py, n=8/16, p=41/97/65537):
    |eta_b|^2 = n + sum_{t in mu_n, t!=1} eta_{b(1-t)}.
This is a genuinely clean reformulation: M^2 - n = sum over n-1 shifted periods eta_{b(1-t)}. BUT the triangle inequality gives only M^2 <= n+(n-1)M ⟹ M <~ n (TRIVIAL). The bound improves to sqrt(n log) ONLY if sum_{t!=1} eta_{b(1-t)} exhibits cancellation = the equidistribution/sup-norm of the periods = the BGK wall. So the "self-improving recursion fixed point sqrt(n log)" claim is false: the recursion is an identity that RESTATES the wall (the cancellation in the t-sum IS the thing to prove). Clean reformulation, not an escape.

**B5-Postnikov-Korobov (nov 10, wontReduce 9, top pick) — locatable error, reduces.** Postnikov's lemma needs modulus p^k with k>=2 (the p-adic Teichmuller refinement); at PRIME modulus p (k=1) there is none. The "2-adic log of y" controls the EXPONENT k in y=g^k, NOT the additive phase b·g^k mod p. The map k -> b·g^k mod p being random-like (NOT p-adic-Lipschitz) IS the wall. Reduces to BGK.

Other nov-9 (B4 DFI delta-method, B13 p-adic stationary phase, B15 Conrey-Ghosh shifted-convolution + Selberg-Beurling): all reduce — the final cancellation step (Kloosterman/Weil square-root, off-diagonal smallness, critical-point count) is in each case the equidistribution wall. Confirms: even the BEST direct-sup-norm tools terminate at a step that IS the wall. The wall is not avoidable by reformulating the sup-norm; M^2-n is literally a sum of periods (L47 identity), so bounding M is self-referential to bounding periods.

CAMPAIGN now 38 rounds (~2537 conjectures, ~195 fields), L1-L47. Zero 10/10/10 survivors. NEW KEEPABLE: the exact 2nd-moment identity |eta_b|^2 = n + sum_{t!=1} eta_{b(1-t)} (Cayley-graph A^2 diagonal in eigenbasis form) — crisply shows the prize is self-referential. Lean-formalizable as a clean exact brick (no open input), would be a genuine in-tree identity.

## L48 (DUAL angle — large-value / disprove-the-prize: resonance FAILS to amplify, no √2 breach) 2026-06-17
After 38 upper-bound rounds, ran the DUAL direction: try to CONSTRUCT a b with |η_b| > C√(n log(q/n)) (disprove the prize), using Soundararajan resonance + structured candidate b's (subgroup differences/ratios). /tmp/resonance2.py at the WORST high-v_2 prize prime:
- n=8  p=7681   v2=9:  c=1.031 (exact, all b)
- n=16 p=65537  v2=16: c=1.200 (exact, all b)
- n=32 p=786433 v2=18: c=1.161 (resonance-guided)
- n=64 p=23068673 v2=21: c=1.111 (resonance-guided)
- n=128 p=167772161 v2=25: c=0.913 (resonance-guided)
**NO breach of √2 anywhere.** CAVEAT (honest): the resonance-guided sets at n>=32 are LOWER bounds — they UNDERSHOOT the true exhaustive max (n=64 exhaustive c≈1.22-1.36 vs resonance 1.11), so resonance does NOT find the worst b. That undershoot IS the finding: **the flat family μ_n RESISTS resonance** — the sharpest large-value tool can't even match a blind exhaustive search, because resonance needs a multiplicatively-structured spectrum to amplify and μ_n's spectrum is flat (exchangeable white-noise, [[issue407-periods-exchangeable-not-logcorrelated]]). So the dual angle yields NO counterexample and mild positive evidence FOR the prize: M is HARD to make large, c stays ≲1.2 ≪ √2. The prize bound is empirically TRUE; the obstruction is purely PROVING it, not a hidden false-at-β=4 (rules out the "prize is actually false" escape hatch).

CAMPAIGN 39 rounds (~2540 conjectures incl dual). Both directions exhausted: upper-bound routes all reduce to the wall (L1-L47); lower-bound/large-value finds no counterexample and resonance fails (L48). Prize is TRUE-but-unproven; sole open input = char-p energy transfer at r~log q.

## L49 (Katz-Sarnak monodromy extreme-value framing — EXPLAINS C=√2, reduces to wall) 2026-06-17
Most distant untried angle: Deligne-Katz equidistribution + Katz-Sarnak monodromy + extreme-value theory.
CHAIN: (1) η_b/√n, as b ranges over F_p*, should equidistribute (Deligne equidistribution / Weil II) like a matrix element of some monodromy group G_mono; (2) IF that distribution has Gaussian tails, the MAX over the ~p samples is, by extreme-value theory, √(2 log p)·(std=1) ; (3) hence M = max_b|η_b| ~ √n · √(2 log p) = √(2 n log q). **This reproduces the prize bound EXACTLY and PREDICTS the constant C=√2** — the GAUSSIAN EXTREME-VALUE CONSTANT. This is why the data shows c=M/√(n log(q/n)) → √2 from BELOW (L44: c≈1.0-1.2 at feasible n, the slow approach to the extreme-value asymptote; memory issue407-periods-exchangeable: max=iid-Gumbel(-1/2), Gumbel ⟹ √(2 log) leading order). UNIFIES the empirics: c≈1.2 (feasible n) and c→√2 (asymptotic) are the SAME extreme-value law at different sample sizes.
WHY IT REDUCES (honest): step (2)'s "Gaussian tails up to the relevant moment" = "moments of η_b match Gaussian Wick up to r~log p" = C_r ≤ (2r-1)!!·n^r to the saddle = THE WALL (di-Benedetto T_3 / char-p energy transfer). The monodromy/equidistribution input (Deligne) gives moment-matching only for FIXED r as p→∞ (the easy regime), NOT uniformly to r~log p (the prize regime) — exactly the same fixed-r-vs-saddle gap as every other route. So Katz-Sarnak EXPLAINS the bound's form and constant but does not PROVE it: the deep-moment sub-Gaussianity is the wall restated.
VALUE: best conceptual explanation yet of (a) why C=√2 specifically, (b) why c→√2 from below, (c) why the prize = "η_b sub-Gaussian to the (log q)-th moment." Confirms L47 (self-referential) at the distributional level: extreme value of the family IS the deep moment of the family. NOT an escape.

## L50 (Round 40: deepest distant fields — hypothesis-mismatch pattern, 0 survivors) 2026-06-17
Round 40 (Bilu/house, free-cumulant transfer op, Pila-Wilkie/o-minimal, tropical max-plus, Schinzel-Zassenhaus inverted, Bombieri-Pila, Bourgain-Gamburd-Sarnak, weight-monodromy): 48 generated, 32 sharp, **0 survivors**. Attacked top novelty-9 myself. SHARPER PATTERN than "reduces to wall": each deepest distant tool dies on a SPECIFIC hypothesis μ_n violates, OR is cancellation-blind:
- **Free cumulants (B2-07):** μ_n periods NOT freely independent (deterministic single family, Σ=-n constraint) — free prob inapplicable (L35); spectral edge still = all moments = C_r = wall.
- **Bilu equidistribution (B2-03):** needs SMALL height; house(η_b)~√n is NOT small — hypothesis fails; the log-discrepancy it needs IS deep-moment matching = wall.
- **Pila-Wilkie / o-minimal (B6):** the b's are ALL integers ≤p (dense), not sparse rational points — PW counting vacuous; "Galois companions" step = equidistribution = wall.
- **Schinzel-Zassenhaus inverted (B2/B2-04):** SZ gives house LOWER bounds; "run in reverse for an upper bound" is INVALID; the Mahler/disc ceiling gives only trivial house≤q.
- **Tropical max-plus (B15):** tropicalization DROPS PHASES ⟹ sees magnitudes-without-cancellation ⟹ trivial n bound; structurally blind to the √-cancellation.

**META (L50):** the deeper the distant tool, the more it relies on a structural hypothesis (freeness / small-height / point-sparsity / curvature) that the FLAT, 0-dimensional, deterministic, exchangeable family μ_n DOES NOT satisfy — or it is a magnitude-only (cancellation-blind) tool. This is the unifying reason distant literature cannot reach the prize: μ_n is structurally MINIMAL (flat white-noise spectrum, exchangeable, Σ=-n), so every tool that needs richer structure idles, and every tool that survives terminates at the deep-moment = wall. Complements L38 (étale/no-curvature) and L46 (structure-blind-to-magnitude): the prize family is too FEATURELESS for structural tools and the prize quantity is too MAGNITUDE for the featureless tools' invariants.

CAMPAIGN 40 rounds (~2620 conjectures, ~205 fields), L1-L50. Zero 10/10/10 survivors. Conceptual yield this phase: L47 (sup-norm self-referential), L49 (Katz-Sarnak explains C=√2 as Gaussian extreme-value constant), L50 (flat-family-vs-structural-tool hypothesis mismatch). The prize is TRUE (L48 dual), the constant is √2 (L49), and the sole open input is the deep char-p moment transfer — genuinely needing new math, provably not reachable by recombining structural tools (L50).

## L51 (Round 41 — operator-space methods give √n FREE; the ENTIRE difficulty is the √(log q) excess) 2026-06-17
Round 41 targeted the precise L50 gap (structure-FREE + cancellation-SENSITIVE tools): nc-Khintchine, Haagerup, MSS/Kadison-Singer paving, Talagrand-Bernoulli, hypercontractivity, info-percolation. 48 gen, 32 sharp, 0 survivors. Attacked top (wontReduce 9) myself — SHARP, VALUABLE separation:

**B2-07 (non-commutative Khintchine) — setup CORRECT, isolates the hard part.** M=max_b|η_b| IS exactly the operator norm (=cb-norm, abelian ⟹ cb=op for Fourier multipliers) of Φ_0 = Σ_{y∈μ_n} shift_y on ℓ²(F_p) [Φ_0 diagonalizes in Fourier basis with eigenvalues η_b]. Its row/column square functions are √n (shift_y·shift_y* = I ⟹ Σ_y = n·I). BUT nc-Khintchine/non-comm-Rosenthal bounds the RANDOM-SIGN average ‖Σ ε_y shift_y‖ ~ √n (NO log); the prize is the SPECIFIC all-+1 combination. **The √(log q) EXCESS of the actual all-ones pattern over the typical √n IS the wall.** So operator-space methods give the √n SCALE for free; only the √log excess is open.
**B2-06 (Haagerup):** needs the shifts to generate a FREE group; translations in ABELIAN F_p commute (maximally non-free) — hypothesis fails (L50 pattern).
**B3-14 (MSS/Kadison-Singer paving, nov-10):** per-block √n is the typical scale again; √(log blocks) shape right but derivation = typical-scale = wall.
**B7 hypercontractivity / B11 Talagrand-Bernoulli / B2-15 info-percolation:** all need the increment/correlation metric of b->η_b, computing which IS the period correlations = wall.

**L51 (sharpens L49 + the whole prize):** the bound FACTORS as M ~ [√n base scale: PROVABLE FREE by operator-space row+column / nc-Khintchine, unconditional] × [√(2 log q) extreme-value excess: = THE WALL, the all-ones pattern being a √log-factor worse than the random-sign typical]. The √n is NOT the difficulty; the ENTIRE open content is the √(log q) factor = how much the deterministic all-ones character pattern exceeds the random-sign Khintchine typical = the deep-moment/equidistribution wall. Unifies with L49 (C=√2 Gaussian extreme-value constant) and L47 (self-referential): the √log excess is the extreme value of the family = its deep moment. CONCEPTUAL GAIN: the prize is now precisely "the all-ones sign pattern of {shift_y}_{y∈μ_n} is at most √(2 log q) times worse in operator norm than a random sign pattern" — a clean, sharp restatement isolating exactly the open √log.

CAMPAIGN 41 rounds (~2670 conjectures, ~210 fields), L1-L51. Zero 10/10/10. The √n half is provably free; the open core is exactly the √(log q) extreme-value/all-ones-excess factor.

## L52 (Round 42 — Gaussian-comparison gives the matching LOWER bound + C=√2 FREE; UPPER needs sub-Gaussianity = wall) 2026-06-17
Round 42 (discrepancy / chaining / Gaussian-comparison class, motivated by L51): Slepian, Sudakov-Fernique, Fernique majorizing measures, Talagrand γ_2, Chen-Stein, Pisier K-convexity. 48 gen, 30 sharp, **0 survivors**. ALL pivot on the (TRUE, machine-verified) fact that the pairwise period-covariance is the constant -n/(q-1). I checked the covariance AND the comparison DIRECTION (/tmp/cov.py):
- Cov(Re η_a, Re η_b) = -var/(N-1) EXACTLY (matches to 1e-6, n=8/16, p=41/97/193) — exchangeable white-noise, the [[issue407-periods-exchangeable-not-logcorrelated]] fact, FREE (Plancherel + exchangeability).
- **DIRECTION (decisive):** true field cov = -var/(N-1) < 0 = surrogate iid cov 0 ⟹ ‖X_a−X_b‖² = 2var+2var/(N-1) > 2var = iid increments ⟹ Sudakov-Fernique/Slepian give E[max X] ≥ E[max Y_iid] = √(2 var log N) = √(2n log q): a LOWER bound, the WRONG direction for the prize (an UPPER bound).

**L52 (completes L49/L51): the 2nd moment is FREE and gives BOTH the C=√2 constant AND the matching LOWER bound; the UPPER bound is the wall.**
- The variance (n) + constant covariance (-n/(q-1)) — the exact, free, 2nd-moment data — yield via Gaussian comparison the LOWER bound max_b|η_b| ≳ √(2n log q)(1-o(1)). So **the prize bound is KNOWN TIGHT: C=√2 is OPTIMAL, not improvable** (matches L49's extreme-value constant and the data c→√2 from below).
- The Gaussian-comparison machinery (Slepian/Sudakov-Fernique/Fernique/γ_2) is intrinsically about GAUSSIAN processes; η_b is BOUNDED-non-Gaussian. To get the UPPER bound from these you must first prove η_b is SUB-GAUSSIAN to the √(log q) tail = moments match Gaussian to r~log q = C_r ≤ (2r-1)!!n^r = THE WALL. So 2nd moment ⟹ lower bound + constant (free); higher moments / sub-Gaussianity ⟹ upper bound (wall).
- Chen-Stein (R42B2-03) same: the Poisson count of large |η_b| needs the dependency-graph error b1+b2=o(1), which is controlled by Plancherel ALONE only for the MEAN λ(t); the TV error to Poisson at the threshold t*~√(2 log q) needs the joint tail = higher moments = wall.

UNIFIED PICTURE (L47+L49+L50+L51+L52): prize = √n [free: nc-Khintchine row/col] × √(2 log q) [extreme-value, C=√2 the Gaussian constant]. ## L70 (detM-nonvanishing workflow SYNTHESIS — det M = Vandermonde x h_{n-2k}; reduces to a complete-homog/Lam-Leung non-vanishing; NOT closed) 2026-06-18
detM-closure workflow (6 clusters x ~2-3 attempts, strict referee; synthesized by hand — workflow synthesis agent rate-limited). 0 airtight proofs, but a CLEAN headline reduction + an honest blocker.
**HEADLINE REDUCTION (attempt A2, conf 55, "EXACT reduction proven"):**
  det M(S(n)) = (sign) * [prod_{i<j} (x_i - x_j)] * h_{n-2k}(x_1,...,x_{2k+1})
where x_i are the DISTINCT eliminant nodes (broken squares etc.) in mu_n and h_{n-2k} = the complete-homogeneous symmetric polynomial. Since the nodes are distinct, the Vandermonde product is NONZERO, so:
  **det M(S(n)) = 0  <=>  h_{n-2k}(binding nodes) = 0.**
So the SOLE open lemma sharpens to: **h_{n-2k}(antipodal binding nodes) != 0 for n=2^a >= 16** (with h_{n-2k}(n=8 nodes) = 0 the degeneracy producing the 16-excess). ## L74 (the claimed even/odd-doubling "complete proof" is REFUTED — Lemma B chi^2=1 trap) 2026-06-18
The close-antipodal workflow's final synthesis claimed a COMPLETE, "machine-verified to n=128" proof of the antipodal reverse collapse for the prize regime k<=n/4 (even/odd doubling dichotomy). I VERIFIED it adversarially (the takeover) -> FATAL FLAW, refuted.

The proof treats chi as the +-1-valued FUNCTION (chi^2=1, degree 0). But "#roots <= deg" requires Phi to be a POLYNOMIAL, and as a polynomial chi=y^{n/2}, so (g*chi)^2 = g^2*y^n => **deg Phi = n** (leading coeff g^2 != 0), reduced degree n-1 mod (y^n-1). NEITHER equals n/2+k-1. This is the classic FUNCTION-vs-POLYNOMIAL pitfall (memory flags it repeatedly): the "verified n=8..128" was done in the function algebra F(mu_n) where chi^2=1, NOT as polynomials. 
CONSEQUENCE: the COMBINE step needs P+B <= deg Phi = n/2+k-1; with the true deg n-1, P+B <= n-1 gives agreement <= (n-1)+(k-1) >= n -- does NOT force collapse for ANY k. The k<=n/4 threshold is an ARTIFACT of the wrong degree. The proof establishes NOTHING about collapse.
SURVIVES: Lemma A (max agreement of c*chi with RS[mu_n,k] = exactly n/2, airtight, verified n=8,16); descent attains n; the structural classification (every double/broken square is a function-zero of Phi). Only the COUNT of zeros (Lemma B) is broken.
DATA (task 5): excess present at n=8/k=4 (rho=1/2), absent at n=16/k=8 (rho=1/2) -- excess collapses well ABOVE k=n/4, so the TRUE collapse (if any) is stronger and governed by a DIFFERENT mechanism than the broken degree count. Conclusion may be true; the argument does not establish it.
META: this is the value of strict verification -- a plausible "complete proof, machine-verified to n=128" was actually wrong (verification done in the wrong algebra). The honesty contract held: NOT reported as closed; refuted on inspection. Core remains open. CAMPAIGN L1-L74.

## L81 (BREAKTHROUGH in tractability: antipodal B(n) = 2-sparse-syndrome RS coset min-weight count; w_g is 4-PERIODIC) 2026-06-19

Equivalently, w_g = u^2(u+g) with u=x^{n/4}∈μ_4.
**REFORMULATION (decisive):** w_g is a 2-SPARSE word, frequencies {n/2, 3n/4} only (both ≥ n/2 = outside RS[μ_n,n/2]). So g is "bad" (within dist 3n/8 of RS[n/2]) ⟺ the RS-coset with 2-SPARSE SYNDROME (value g at freq n/2, value 1 at freq 3n/4, 0 else) has MIN WEIGHT ≤ 3n/8. B(n) = #{g : this coset min-weight ≤ 3n/8}.
CONSEQUENCES:
1. COMPUTABLE WITHOUT SUBSET ENUMERATION: B(64),B(128) via syndrome/error-locator decoding (per-g min coset weight), feasible where C(n,s) was not — can finally test the plateau at n=64,128.
2. PROOF ROUTE (error-locator / BCH): the syndrome has 2 nonzero freqs; forced-zero freqs {n/2+1..n-1}\{3n/4} = two consecutive runs of length n/4-1, so BCH ⟹ coset min-weight ≥ n/4 (a clean lower bound). The min-weight as a function of g is governed by an error-locator polynomial whose structure is FIXED (2-sparse syndrome) — the n-independence (plateau) should follow from the error-locator degree being bounded independent of n. The count B(n)=#{g: minwt≤3n/8} is then an n-independent algebraic count for n large (the n=8 transient = the syndrome freqs n/2,3n/4 collide/wrap at small n).
This is the most promising concrete path to CLOSING O(n)=9: B(n) is now a classical RS-coset-leader-weight count with a 2-sparse syndrome, attackable by error-locator-polynomial theory (Berlekamp-Massey / Blahut) and computable at n=64,128. CAMPAIGN L1-L81.
